<text>My husband, myself, and our two year old son all had our first appointments here in the last week.  We drive over 20 minutes to get to the office but it is SO worth it.  Every single person on staff, from the receptionist to the hygienists to both Dr. Sasha and Dr. Sara are friendly, welcoming, professional, helpful, courteous, detailed... everything you could ask for.
For my first visit, they did a 3D scan of my entire head, which allowed Dr. Sasha to see everything from my teeth to my sinuses and my jaw.  This was after I had the opportunity to sit down with him in his office and just give him my background, any past issues, etc. AND I got a tour of the office by one of the hygienists.  The cleaning is scheduled for a different appointment than the initial exam so they can make sure to schedule the right amount of time for you.  I consider this very professional!  There was little to no waiting time - very efficient.

I took my son in the next day.  They have separate adult and kids days.  When I came in on the "kids" day, there were kids shows on tv, foam letters and numbers to play with, and I think even a video game off to the side.  This was my son's first "real" dentist visit (he had been once before, but just sat on my lap and the dentist just looked at his teeth and poked around with his fingers).  Dr. Sasha and the hygienist were so friendly and talked to him about his letters and numbers before beginning.  Then he got to sit in the "special chair" and as they leaned him back, there was a TV on the ceiling for him to watch!  She was able to brush, floss, and paint flouride on his teeth.  I was able to talk with her for several minutes about some questions, and my son wanted to explore the office so Dr. Sasha asked the front receptionist to watch him so I didn't have to keep an eye on him.  At the end, he got stickers from the prize box AND a balloon!  More importantly than that,  I feel more confident with how to help take care of my 2 year old's teeth at home because of the detailed instructions that were both explained and modeled for me there.

I cannot recommend this office enough!  Three amazing experiences in the last week (I'll let my husband write his own review).  We look forward to returning every six months!< /text><Rating>5</Rating><Response>None<//Response><user_id>114767791985743214997< /user_id>< GmapID>

I have only been a patient at New Generation Dentistry and Dr. Sasha's for a few months now.  My initial consultation was very professional and all of my concerns were addressed.  The cleaning was scheduled a few weeks after that and I was very impressed with the facilities, tools, and equipment. At first it was a strange sensation, but definitely could tell a difference afterwards.

Dr. Sasha was also great with an issue I had with my night guard.  I had a new night guard made, but was unhappy with the softness at night.  When I showed up for a follow up appointment, Dr. Sasha had already called the company and had a harder night guard ready for me, even before I had discussed my concern directly with him!!! <Text>While the outside and name may make it sound like upscale lounge, that fantasy dies as soon as you walk in.

The beer and wine selection are on par with most bars but the liquors available were terrible. If you're looking for quality this place is one to avoid. There is also no cocktail menu or bartenders that know how make basic one (mine had to look up what a tequila sunrise was)

The atmosphere is cheap, dated, and not maintained that well. It's small and usually filled with your all-day drinkers. There is one pool table and two arcade games from the 80's. This place is definitely not a lounge and has virtually no cocktails. This is very much on the do not recommend list.</Text>< pics>

<user_id>115473318031040300426</user_id><username>Steven Kenyon<//username><time>1544392256909</time>< rating>
5<//rating>
< text>
This is such an amazing place!! They offer Sporting clays and skeet course.  If you are not familiar, sporting clays are like golf but with shotguns.  The sporting clays range is soo much fun!  You walk to each station (they do rent golf carts) and push a button to launch a clay.  You can work as a team with one person "pulling" the clays or by yourself using the system in delay mode.  You can rent or bring your own gun, can also buy ammo (wal-mart has better deals on ammo).  Each station is unique and you pay by the clay, so if you want you can just stay at a given station all day (making allowances for others who want to play through.)< /text>

<review>Bang Bang Bang!

Definitely a great place for a date (depending on the girl) or a surprise date for a guy! What guy/girl doesn't like to shoot and let out some steam?

My friend suggested this place and at first I was skeptical because I was afraid of the recoil from previous experiences with shooting. I'm glad he's a "pro" cause he definitely knew what he was doing. He chose the shotgun with the least amount of recoil. He also warned me about how I would get some bruising on my shoulder from holding the shotgun. Next time, I should bring some shoulder pads or a makeshift shoulder pad.

There are about 20 courses, which is a lot! Each course has their own uniqueness to it. You can even rent a go cart to drive around to the courses. The clay birdies that roll on the ground are usually called "rabbits" which is cute. You can spend from a couple of hours or a whole day shooting.

In our group of 6, we shared about 300 bullets and even had bullets left over. The unopened left overs, you can return. You pay after you finishing shooting. Each of us paid about less $40.

I'll definitely come back, with the right shoes, a hat, shades and my makeshift shoulder pad.<//review>< time>
1429665847237<//time>

<Rate>1< /Rate>< text>
If you are not 100% certain on the final destination for a loved one to be laid to rest, I suggest that you do not use Valhalla as an interim location. For cremation services in particular, you would be better off using a local (non-corporation) establishment. They charge large fees for refrigeration, even if it was only for five days. I understand that they need to make money, but transportation for less than 20 miles and refrigeration for five days should not have totaled $1,520. After research, the same services between four other locations would average $1,100 to $1,200. When the provider I chose went to retrieve my father, they did not budge on the $1,520. At the end of they day, Valhalla is a corporation, and their number one objective is to make money, not be reasonable. Go there for yourself to see.</text>

< Review>
I felt from day one that they knew they had me over a barrel. Everything was so outrageously expensive (one ex: $500 dollars to drive my son from the chapel to graveside - no more than 20-30 yards)! I constantly felt like I was being kicked when I was already down!!! Things haven't gotten much better in the two years since the funeral. There have been numerous issues with groundskeeping spraying the flower arrangements with grass and dirt due to carelessness, and birthday decorations that were thrown away AFTER I checked with the front office if it was in keeping with their standards. Most recently, there were my son's flower service flowers that weren't ordered when they should've been, and his flower service flowers that were thrown away when they shouldn't have been! When I tried to get help after I discovered his flowers were thrown out, I felt like a fly that everyone was just trying to shoo away, saying "someone will call you on Monday". When I quietly (because a service was being held nearby) expressed my upset feelings to someone named Christina, and walked away towards my son's grave, she sent a security guard to tell me to leave them alone! I had told her that once they have your money, they don't really care about you, and that people should know about that.
Alfredo was very nice and helped me get flowers put back down a couple days later, and Isela tried to help me before the flowers were taken, by re-ordering  my son's flower service, and assuring me that his current flowers could remain an extra month. But someone else, who didn't know what Isela had told me, threw them away anyway.  Maybe it doesn't seem like a big deal to some of the people there, maybe they think "it's just flowers lady",  but when there's nothing left I can do for my son but keep a token of my love for him on his grave, it's a really big deal to me. I do NOT recommend Pierce Brothers!!!< /Review>

I started training at San Diego Brazilian Jiu-Jitsu in 2007. I have explored other dojo's both locally and across multiple states. I have yet to find a sensei who genuinely cares more for his students and their families than Paulo does. His experience in both Jiu-jitsu and Judo is second to none. He also offers Muay Thai classes among others. If you're seeking a place for your child to safely learn self defense, balance, respect then search no further. The diversity of the students within each class is also an amazing thing. You won't feel over whelmed as a new student and there is also plenty of people to challenge you if that's your thing. Everyone there is always willing to help in literally every aspect you can think of. I've seen professional fighters come to take classes and learn something new, military personnel, nutritionist, etc. I currently live just outside Yosemite National Park and took it upon myself to drive the 5.5 hour long drive just to take a few classes and be surrounded with my 2nd family. Thank you so much Paulo for all of your teachings. Not only on the mat but as a person as well. You have always been my sensei and will forever be regardless of how far away I live. I will see you soon! Oos</Review>

< resp>

<Review>I've been a student here for almost four years.  When you step into the dojo you are immediately welcomed by Sensei Paulo, Sensei Adam, Katia, Jesus or one of the staff.  This is the place where you can comfortably learn the martial arts in a focused, family friendly environment.  If you are a beginner, it won't take long for you to see that this is not a macho, testosterone driven, "knuckle dragger" environment full of bolstered egos.  You will be brought into the fold and given the appropriate attention so you can quickly learn the basics in order to move forward in the arts.  If you are an intermediate or experienced practitioner, you will be challenged with players of all levels.  Sparring competition is intense with focus on learning and safety at all times.  Respect for your partners in this aspect is a must and part of the beauty of the discipline of the arts.

This place is great for the kiddos too!  The kids program is excellent.  I have two young boys and judo and jiu jitsu has helped them gain confidence and coordination.  For moms and dads worried about turning their kids into bullies, I can tell you that you can expect quite the opposite.  The arts are not taught for this purpose and your kids will learn to respect others.

For the ladies out there, be assured that you are absolutely welcome here too!  There are many women involved in Muay Thai, Jiu Jitsu and Judo.  Respect is given to all students and the women are no exception.  This is a safe environment for all.

I don't personally take part in the Studio Brazil workouts or Muay Thai but I have seen and spoken to those that do.  All that I have spoken too are very satisfied with the experience and the workouts.  They work hard and it shows.

So get in here and become part of the experience, the arts, and the SDBJJ family!

< review>
Just took my first day here. I used to train at a very reputable gym down in Miramar, but I live in Escondido and the commute there was an issue I would like to avoid. I used to train 2 years ago but am very picky on where I'm going to invest my time, health, and money into a gym membership. For the past 3 weeks I have been taking free trial classes all over San Diego county. Mostly NORTH San Diego County. Now let me tell you, ALL the decent gyms are down in San Diego. In North County there are literally none. There was one gym in Oceanside that I liked but again, I wanted to avoid a long commute. San Diego Brazilian Jiu-Jitsu & Mixed Martial Arts to me, is THE ONLY amazing gym in Northeast San Diego County, maybe even in the entire north county. I have been looking for an emphasis on technique for Muay Thai, Jiu-Jitsu, and Judo. A lot of other gyms will focus more on "fitness". The programs incorporate both. Exactly what I wanted. If I wanted to go to a gym that focuses on fitness, I might as well go to a generic LA Fitness or 24 hour gym.

Now let's discuss my first day here. It is located in San Marcos which is a relatively safe city. I walked in to a beautifully spacious establishment and most of all....SANITARY AND CLEAN. I walked down to the morning Muay Thai class and was invited by friendly students and most of all a friendly coach. The students and coach automatically pushed me and motivated me to the point where I automatically felt the family oriented vibes the gym emits. We warmed up, and being out of shape for 2 years, they kept pushing me with positive remarks. After we started to work on technique and Jesus, the coach, was thorough and very hands on working with us. When class was done, it ended with positivity and embedded an amazing first impression into my brain. I knew that this gym was the one.

The owner, is big time. He is highly certified and has so much experience under his belt for Judo and BJJ that it's overwhelming. He still competes to! The gym has been one of the most longest standing gyms in San Diego. They're doing something right. I initially came for the Muay Thai classes but it looks like I will be committing to Jiu-Jitsu and Judo just as much as my love for striking.

If you are a picky student looking for technique and fitness. Your gym is here.</review>

< review>
The Alley accommodated us for my friend's bachelorette party on a Saturday night. They let us come in when they opened (6pm) and decorate for the party to reserve our location by the dance floor and live band. They also let us keep our cupcakes in the fridge. We arrived at 9pm where everyone from the bouncer to the bartenders made us feel very special since it was the bride-to-be's special night! At the end of the night the bride was hungry and they (the waitress and bouncer) offered to walk next door to pick up a pizza we ordered, HOW kind and seriously above and beyond it was. They went out of their way to make us all feel special and welcomed. The music was awesome, and we liked how they had the live band but then also played dancing music in between too. I would recommend going here to anyone! Thank you for the great service!< /review>

On multiple occasions, I had Mitchell and/or different team members contact me for documents that I had already uploaded into their online portal days ago and those documents hadn't been reviewed in that time; they were just sitting there. Without my and my husband's consent, Mitchell tried to charge us a fee in order to lower our interest rate. He acted like he was the one who was able to give us such a great interest rate, but in reality, we were the ones who gave ourselves the lower interest rate, because he was charging us to buy points, which is something that we had not discussed or agreed to. On our loan disclosure, he had additional fees and no lender credit towards us. When we questioned him on this, he said, "Well, I have a company to run and employees to pay." He did not seem to care that as his clients (who have stable jobs and incredible credit scores) we have a family to care for. We decided to consult with another lender Ben Swett (who is amazing and we HIGHLY recommend), and he pointed out all of the questionable items on our loan disclosure. Ben helped us negotiate with Mitchell, so that we can get a better deal. Something I feel we shouldn't have had to do in the first place as his clients. Also, from the beginning, I disclosed to Mitchell during a phone call and on our loan application that we would be gifted some money from my parents. He said that was fine and didn't give me any further instructions. We deposited the check from my parents, and it wasn't until we were close to wrapping everything up, Mitchell told us that we need a copy of the check, which we didn't have. We spoke with our bank, and they told us that our lender could retrieve a copy of the check faster than we could, so we emailed the bank's instructions on how to attain a copy of the check to Mitchell and his team. Mitchell called my husband and alluded to the fact that he can't get a copy of the check, because it was illegal for him to do it, even though our bank said he could get it. Two of Mitchell's team members contacted me and asked me to get a copy of the check, and that's when I finally told them of my dissatisfaction with their service and how they're constantly making us jump through hoops instead of helping us throughout this process. Not once has Mitchell apologized to me or my husband for his lack of professionalism and reluctance to help us. He continued to act cheerful and go on as if nothing was wrong, and he would repeatedly say how he's worked so hard to get us a great deal, but at that point, it all felt very fake and narcissistic of him. Another thing, through the majority of this process, he only contacted me and would leave my husband out on emails and texts. I addressed the issue by telling him that he needs to include my husband in all communication, because we're buying the house together and my husband needs to be in the know of what's happening. Mitchell continued to only contact me even if it was my husband who was reaching out to him via text or phone call. I'm definitely not satisfied with Mitchell's actions and service.<//Text>

<text>It was a pleasure working with Steve! Funny story, I actually chose him randomly from the AP Mortgage website, looked at everyone's pictures and thought, "oh, he looks like a nice guy." AP Mortgage was the preferred lender for the property I purchased and unlike other lender websites, I didn't see a way to just apply for a loan on their website. There was just a form to fill in your information to have someone contact you to give you a quote. Well, I waited a day and no one had contacted me other than an email saying someone will reach out, so me being impatient, clicked around the website and found out I can send in an application after selecting a loan officer and visiting their page!

Anyway, Steve was great! He has experience working in this field for quite some time, so he was watching the market to get me a good rate. If anything important comes up that needs to be done right away, he always calls. Everything was a breeze, no huge hiccups. He takes the time to explain things in ways I can understand, since this is my 1st home, I didn't know much of the process at all.

I went into the process with certain expectations and knowing I would need to provide alot of documentation, so I think I already had most of what was normally required. Due to my personal circumstances, Steve suggested I provide more work history to show consistency and a letter with explanation of gaps. I thought it was a great idea to be extra thorough to submit all of it in one big package! I have read other's experiences where they feel annoyed that they have to keep submitting more because the underwriter keeps requesting additional information and I did not feel any frustrations regarding that at all.
